# Organelles & Functions
## [[Cytoplasmic Membrane\|Cell Membrane]]
- Found in all cells
- Also called the *[[200 Science/210 Biology/Unit 1.2 - Biomolecules/1.2.4 - Lipids#^868bba\|phospholipid]] bilayer* or *plasma membrane*
- **Barrier that regulates what enters & exits the cell**
- Composed of 3 of the 4 biomolecules
	- Carbohydrate ID tags
	- Protein transport molecules
	- Lipid Bilayer
![Cell membrane.jpeg](/img/user/Files/Cell%20membrane.jpeg)
## [[Cell Wall\|Cell Wall]]
- Found in [[200 Science/210 Biology/Unit 1.1 - Cell Structure & Function, and Viruses/1.1.4 -  Viruses vs. Prokaryotes#Prokaryotes\|Prokaryotes]] & [[200 Science/210 Biology/Unit 1.1 - Cell Structure & Function, and Viruses/1.1.5 - Prokaryotes vs. Eukaryotes#Eukaryotes\|Eukaryotes]]
- **Made of cellulose (carbohydrate) in plants**
- Added layer of protection
- **Gives cells strong, rigid structure**
![Plant_cell_wall_diagram-en.svg-58a8766c3df78c345bdc5df3.png](/img/user/Files/Plant_cell_wall_diagram-en.svg-58a8766c3df78c345bdc5df3.png)
## [[Centrioles\|Centrioles]]
- Found in **Animal Cells**
- Paired
- Located in [[Cytoplasm\|Cytoplasm]], near nucleus
- **Organize microtubules in the centromere**
- **Organize the mitotic spindle**
![Centrioles.jpeg](/img/user/Files/Centrioles.jpeg)
## [[Chloroplasts\|Chloroplasts]]
- Found in Plant Cells 
- **Site of [[photosynthesis\|photosynthesis]]**
- **Contains high levels of chlorophyll**
- **Converts sunlight energy into chemical energy** *(glucose)*
- Green

## [[Flashcards/Science/Biology/Cilia\|Cilia]] & [[Flagella\|Flagella]]
- Found in [[200 Science/210 Biology/Unit 1.1 - Cell Structure & Function, and Viruses/1.1.4 -  Viruses vs. Prokaryotes#Prokaryotes\|Prokaryotes]] & [[200 Science/210 Biology/Unit 1.1 - Cell Structure & Function, and Viruses/1.1.5 - Prokaryotes vs. Eukaryotes#Eukaryotes\|Eukaryotes]]
- **Cell Movement**
- **[[Flashcards/Science/Biology/Cilia\|Cilia]] move back & forth**
- **[[Flagella\|Flagella]] move like a propeller**
- Powered by [[Periodic Table of Elements/And Compounds/Adenosine Triphosphate\|Adenosine Triphosphate]]
![Cillia-Flagella.jpeg](/img/user/Files/Cillia-Flagella.jpeg)
## [[Cytoplasm\|Cytoplasm]] 
- Found in **all cells:** [[200 Science/210 Biology/Unit 1.1 - Cell Structure & Function, and Viruses/1.1.4 -  Viruses vs. Prokaryotes#Prokaryotes\|Prokaryotes]] & [[200 Science/210 Biology/Unit 1.1 - Cell Structure & Function, and Viruses/1.1.5 - Prokaryotes vs. Eukaryotes#Eukaryotes\|Eukaryotes]] 
- Majority of the intercellular environment
- Where metabolic reactions occur
- [[Periodic Table of Elements/And Compounds/Dihydrogen Oxide\|Water]], salts, & [[Flashcards/Science/Biology/Proteins\|Proteins]]
![Cytoplasm.png](/img/user/Files/Cytoplasm.png)
## [[Flashcards/Science/Biology/Cytoskeleton\|Cytoskeleton]]
- Found in [[200 Science/210 Biology/Unit 1.1 - Cell Structure & Function, and Viruses/1.1.4 -  Viruses vs. Prokaryotes#Prokaryotes\|Prokaryotes]] & [[200 Science/210 Biology/Unit 1.1 - Cell Structure & Function, and Viruses/1.1.5 - Prokaryotes vs. Eukaryotes#Eukaryotes\|Eukaryotes]]
- Cell Structure 
- Filament & Tubules in Cytoplasm
- Determine shape of cell
![Cytoskeleton-1.png](/img/user/Files/Cytoskeleton-1.png)
## [[Flashcards/Science/Biology/Golgi Apparatus\|Golgi Bodies]] 
- Found in [[200 Science/210 Biology/Unit 1.1 - Cell Structure & Function, and Viruses/1.1.5 - Prokaryotes vs. Eukaryotes#Eukaryotes\|Eukaryotes]]
- Process & package [[Flashcards/Science/Biology/Proteins\|Proteins]] & [[Flashcards/Science/Biology/Lipids\|Lipids]]
- Final folding of [[Flashcards/Science/Biology/Proteins\|Proteins]]
- Directional
	- Cis Face  vesicles enter 
	- Trans face  vesicles exit
![Golgi-apparatus-complex-modification-proteins-role-cell.jpg.webp](/img/user/Files/Golgi-apparatus-complex-modification-proteins-role-cell.jpg.webp)
## [[Lysosomes\|Lysosomes]]
- Found in [[200 Science/210 Biology/Unit 1.1 - Cell Structure & Function, and Viruses/1.1.5 - Prokaryotes vs. Eukaryotes#Eukaryotes\|Eukaryotes]]
- Digestive system of the cell
- Break down material brought into cell
- Break down worn out organelles
- Leads apoptosis
## [[200 Science/210 Biology/Unit 1.1 - Cell Structure & Function, and Viruses/1.1.6 - Plants vs. Animals#Mitochondria\|Mitochondria]] 
- Found in [[200 Science/210 Biology/Unit 1.1 - Cell Structure & Function, and Viruses/1.1.5 - Prokaryotes vs. Eukaryotes#Eukaryotes\|Eukaryotes]]
- Site of cellular respiration 
- Powerhouse of the cell
- Converts glucose to [[Periodic Table of Elements/And Compounds/Adenosine Triphosphate\|Adenosine Triphosphate]]
## [[Nucleus\|Nucleus]] 
### Nuclear Envelope
- Found in [[200 Science/210 Biology/Unit 1.1 - Cell Structure & Function, and Viruses/1.1.5 - Prokaryotes vs. Eukaryotes#Eukaryotes\|Eukaryotes]]
- Membrane around the [[Nucleus\|nucleus]]
- Separate nuclear content, [[200 Science/210 Biology/Unit 1.2 - Biomolecules/Deoxyribonucleic Acid\|Deoxyribonucleic Acid]] from the [[Cytoplasm\|Cytoplasm]]
- Two lipid bilayer membranes
	- Inner
	- Outer
### Nuclear Pore
- Found in [[200 Science/210 Biology/Unit 1.1 - Cell Structure & Function, and Viruses/1.1.5 - Prokaryotes vs. Eukaryotes#Eukaryotes\|Eukaryotes]]
- Channel in nuclear envelope 
- Provides access to the [[Nucleus\|nucleus]] 
- Regulate transport of [[Flashcards/Science/Biology/Proteins\|Proteins]] and [[200 Science/210 Biology/Unit 1.2 - Biomolecules/Ribonucleic Acid\|RNA]] across the nuclear envelope
### Nucleolus
- Found in [[200 Science/210 Biology/Unit 1.1 - Cell Structure & Function, and Viruses/1.1.5 - Prokaryotes vs. Eukaryotes#Eukaryotes\|Eukaryotes]]
- Located inside the [[Nucleus\|nucleus]] 
- Produce and assemble the cells [[Ribosomes\|ribosomes]]
- Ribosomal genes are transcribed
## [[Ribosomes\|Ribosomes]]
- Found in [[200 Science/210 Biology/Unit 1.1 - Cell Structure & Function, and Viruses/1.1.4 -  Viruses vs. Prokaryotes#Prokaryotes\|Prokaryotes]] & [[200 Science/210 Biology/Unit 1.1 - Cell Structure & Function, and Viruses/1.1.5 - Prokaryotes vs. Eukaryotes#Eukaryotes\|Eukaryotes]]
- Made of two separate subunits that come together
- Made of [[200 Science/210 Biology/Unit 1.2 - Biomolecules/Ribonucleic Acid\|RNA]] & [[Flashcards/Science/Biology/Proteins\|Proteins]]
- Site of [[protein synthesis\|protein synthesis]]
- Converts genetic code (mRNA) into an amino acid sequence (protein)
## [[Rough Endoplasmic Reticulum\|Rough Endoplasmic Reticulum]]
- Found in [[200 Science/210 Biology/Unit 1.1 - Cell Structure & Function, and Viruses/1.1.5 - Prokaryotes vs. Eukaryotes#Eukaryotes\|Eukaryotes]]
- Helps in protein production 
	- Production
	- Folding
	- Quality Control
	- Dispatch
- Located right outside the nucleus
## [[Smooth Endoplasmic Reticulum\|Smooth Endoplasmic Reticulum]]
- Found in [[200 Science/210 Biology/Unit 1.1 - Cell Structure & Function, and Viruses/1.1.5 - Prokaryotes vs. Eukaryotes#Eukaryotes\|Eukaryotes]]
- Helps in lipid production
	- Phospholipids
	- Cholesterol
	- Steroid Hormones
- Metabolism of [[Flashcards/Science/Biology/Carbohydrates\|Carbohydrates]]
- Located right outside the nucleus
## [[Vacuoles\|Vacuoles]] 
- Found in [[200 Science/210 Biology/Unit 1.1 - Cell Structure & Function, and Viruses/1.1.5 - Prokaryotes vs. Eukaryotes#Eukaryotes\|Eukaryotes]]
- Hold solution & materials in the cell
- Stores [[Periodic Table of Elements/And Compounds/Dihydrogen Oxide\|water]] and other materials
- Plant Cells - Large
- Animal Cells - Small
